<username>Joseph Valdez<//username>< Time>
1592084613932</Time>
<rate>4</rate>< Text>
Authentic, cultural atmosphere. Good portions. Good price. Pretty good quality compared to shops of it's calibre. Most locals are aware that a lot of taco shops aren't too far from another in terms of how good they are. There's too many here that are long time features of the SD culinary landscape so most shops over 5 or 10 years old are legit. You'll also find out that each has a particular menu item that is significantly better than the competition too. This one is definitely the spot for surf n' turf fries in the rancho SD area hands down. Consistently good in my experience. El Toro off Meadowbrook offers better surf n turf, but not as consistently. They also offer beer and wine so come with an appetite and leave with an altogether satisfied experience.</Text>

< Review>
I've been coming here since the 1980s back when they were over by the closed PO Box room and next to a pet store, same lot different building. Later fond memories of their sit-down restaurant which is now the cell phone store next door, I believe a daughter or wife ran that area. Often talked to Mr Sorrentino and his family, complained direct to the old man when they changed the pizza crust way back when to it's current form, used to be closer to Filippi's crust which is San Diego famous but he had a good reason for the change (oven blowers clogged with flour). Nowadays the food can be somewhat inconsistent due to different employee owner operators or whatever's going on, still good and still five stars. Used to be the absolute best Italian food anywhere so far as I'm concerned, had Italian all over the world and Sorrentino's New York immigrant neighborhood style is still the best and most authentic (which might be considered bland in certain cases) that you're going to get in Clairemont.</Review>

<gmap_id>0x808f9d88bbd2edb5:0xf4923b131e8ac2f9<//gmap_id><username>Eric Data</username><Resp>{'time': 1578531917726, 'text': "Wow! Thank you Eric for your wonderful and detailed review. I'm not a golfer, and it's rare that you would find me at a golf course, until now.

Last Friday my family gathered here for a celebration of life lunch.  Why did we choose Par3?  It's because we heard that it is a new restaurant by Alicia the owner and Chef of Three Craft Kitchen in Downtown San Mateo.

Let's start with something rare for the San Mateo, Burlingame area, lots of free parking!!   You can't beat not having to pay for meters, or searching for parking spaces.

Once we walked into the restaurant, it had a new fresh modern feel.  Wood floors,  new tables, new chairs, big screen tv's, long and inviting bar, so much to mention, and to top it all off, large windows all across the restaurant that provided beautiful views of the golf course from almost every table.

We were greeted immediately by the staff that asked if we wanted to enjoy our lunch inside, or outside in the patio area.  Being a pet friendly  automatically gets a star, we chose to sit inside.

Our group started off with drinks, which they have a ton of beers on tap, both local craft and the other favorite large company brands.   They also have a full bar with a large cocktail menu, with Mojitos and other signature cocktails.  Me personally, I ordered beer =)

We then went into appetizers, our group ordered the Bacon Bites, Pulled Pork Nachos, Pizza, and Chicken Wings.  Everything was delicious and the portions were pretty big!

For lunch, I had a Cheeseburger.  The burger was cooked perfect to my liking, but the highlight was the type of bread they used. It was a soft brioche type sourdough?  I dunno, but it was awesome!  Along with my burger I chose french fries which were perfectly cooked, and perfectly seasoned.  What is perfect fries?  Perfect temperature, and perfect crispyness. Crispyness isn't word, but you get the picture =)

The rest of our table ordered the Adobo Pulled Pork Tacos, the Tuna Melt, the Tri-Tip Dip, and the Salmon Burger.

We were so stuffed, and comfortable, we didn't want to leave.  After lunch we shared an ice cream dessert and ordered an Irish Coffee, Mexican Coffee, and Keoke Coffee.

Irish Coffee had Jameson Whiskey, the Mexican Coffee and Tequila, and the Keoke I think had Brandy?  All 3 of them were excellent and is a MUST for anyone who love coffee liqueurs!

A few more things that I want to add about Par3 is they have a large Banquet Room for meetings, events, parties, and weddings.

I also noticed they have games on the patio lawn, corn hole, and another game that looks like a lawn version of beer pong.  They also have a fireplace out there too.  The next time I visit, I definitely plan to drink a few beers outside and play the lawn games!

Service was top notch, and one more last thing that is the kicker, the prices were super, and I mean SUPER affordable for where you're at.  You would expect to pay double, being on a golf course, and in such a nice modern classy restaurant.  BIG THANK YOU to the owners!!!

Bottomline, glad we chose Par3, our family loved it, and we look forward to our next visit.  I might even start to play golf, well probably just the driving range and putting lawn =)<//review>

< Review>
One of the few places that's still open during pandemic in this plaza. Therefore, parking is a breeze nowadays, as compared to pre-Covid.
Their egg rolls still taste pretty good, but the disappointment is in the shrinking size for all their signature food items (egg rolls, shrimp balls, sesame balls, etc).
I expected the prices to creep up every time I visit, but I didn't expect the portion sizes to shrink this time around. I understand the current economical situation is not ideal, but I was shocked by what I brought home.
Let's all get through this together, and come out the other side stronger and better.<//Review>

< review>
Love the egg rolls and the sauce it comes with!! They have other Asian dishes but the egg rolls are the best. The only thing that really bothers me about King Eggroll is they are so disorganized when it comes to phone orders. I'll call and hour or two ahead, and tell them I want this many egg rolls, and will be in at a certain time. Well, when I get there, instead of a quick payment and grabbing my food to go, they make me grab a ticket and wait.  What's the point of calling in ahead, leave my name and then wait for a while. The wait time can be anywhere between 15 minutes to a whole hour. And I've ordered at several different King Eggroll and they all treat phone orders the same as people who walk in: grab a ticket and wait. I highly recommend coming in and order your food and just expect a half hour wait. If your order comes is ready in a few minutes great, but don't be surprised if it takes longer than 30 minutes (especially on popular days like playoff games, holidays, big pay per view fights, etc).<//review>
